<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нагнетать.html>нагнета́ть</a> (25390)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">нагнет-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nagnet-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нагнетать.html>нагнета́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nagnetátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">нагнести́</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pump, to pressurize, to inflate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to aggravate, to exacerbate (negative emotions)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наговаривать.html>нагова́ривать</a> (22594)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наговорить.html>наговори́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nagovorítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наговаривать.html>нагова́ривать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nagovárivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наговорить.html>наговори́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to record, to read for recording, to have one's reading recorded</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to slander
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нечего.html>не́чего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:наговаривать.html>нагова́ривать</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">néčevo na menjá <b>nagovárivatʹ</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">don't tell lies about me!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***наговорить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наговорить.html>наговори́ть</a> (10011)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">govorítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наговорить.html>наговори́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nagovorítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наговаривать.html>нагова́ривать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to record, to read for recording, to have one's reading recorded</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to slander</li>
<li>to say, to tell
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наговорить.html>наговори́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:глупость.html>глу́постей</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nagovorítʹ</b> glúpostej</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to say a lot of silly things</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наговорить.html>наговори́ть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́го</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неприятный.html>неприя́тного</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nagovorítʹ</b> komú-libo mnógo neprijátnovo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">tell smb a lot of unpleasant things</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="этнографическое">этногр.</span>, <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="региональное">рег.</span>, <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:шептать.html>шепча́</a> знахарские <a href = vnd.unilang:заклинание.html>заклина́ния</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:призвать.html>призва́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> что-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:волшебный.html>волше́бную</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:магический.html>маги́ческую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́лу</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:наговорить.html>Наговори́ть</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>во́ду</a>. </span></li>
</ul></li>

</ol>
<h4><span id=".D0.A1.D0.B8.D0.BD.D0.BE.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.BC.D1.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Синонимы"><a href = vnd.unilang:синоним.html>Сино́нимы</a></span></h4>
<ol><li>-</li>
<li>наклеветать, оговарить, <a href = vnd.unilang:обвинить.html>обвини́ть</a>, очернить</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нагонять.html>нагоня́й</a> (22389)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нагонять.html>нагоня́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nagonjáj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нагонять.html>нагоня́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нагоняй.html>нагоня́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нагоняй.html>нагоня́ев</a></b>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> telling-off, rating, scolding

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получить.html>получи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нагонять.html>нагоня́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">polučitʹ nagonjaj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get a scolding; get into hot water; get it in the neck</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нагонять.html>нагоня́ть</a> (17859)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гонять.html>гоня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gonjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***наготове.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наготове.html>нагото́ве</a> (10886)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">гото́ве</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gotóve</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with the second element having the form of a prepositional singular of a nonexistent noun based on the verb <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:готовить.html>гото́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gotóvitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наготове.html>нагото́ве</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nagotóve</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>at call, in readiness, ready, prepared, on the lookout
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>держа́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:наготове.html>нагото́ве</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">deržátʹ <b>nagotóve</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to keep in readiness</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:награда.html>награ́да</a> (3566)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">нагаро́да</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">naharóda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">нагоро́да</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nahoróda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which were inherited from Old East Slavic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:награда.html>награ́да</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nagráda</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:награда.html>награ́ды</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:награда.html>награ́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:награда.html>награ́д</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>reward (something of value given in return for an act)</li>
<li>award</li>
<li>decoration</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:награждённый.html>награждённый</a> (5974)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:награждённый.html>награждённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nagraždjónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наградить.html>награди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nagradítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нагревать.html>нагрева́ть</a> (20641)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нагреть.html>нагре́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nagrétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нагревать.html>нагрева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nagrevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нагреть.html>нагре́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to heat, to warm</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to swindle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мошенник.html>моше́нник</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нагревать.html>нагрева́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:клиент.html>клие́нтов</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mošénnik <b>nagrevájet</b> klijéntov.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">A con artist swindles the clients.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to heat, warm</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:греть.html>греть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gretʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***нагреть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нагреть.html>нагре́ть</a> (8808)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:греть.html>греть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gretʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нагреть.html>нагре́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nagrétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нагревать.html>нагрева́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to heat, to warm
<dl><dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:греть.html>греть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gretʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to swindle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:незнакомец.html>незнако́мец</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нагреть.html>нагре́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сто.html>сто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рубль.html>рубле́й</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Neznakómec <b>nagrél</b> menjá na sto rubléj.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">A stranger <b>swindled</b> me out of a hundred rubles.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нагреть.html>нагре́в</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nagrév</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
